msg:Facilities: parking lot, gym, swimming pool, restaurant, bar are all available. It is close to Nanhu Park and the transportation is very convenient.

Hygiene: The sanitation from the lobby to the room is very good. The cleaning lady will knock on the door at around 10 o'clock in the morning to ask if you need cleaning service. It is very considerate. If not, you can press the "Do Not Disturb" light.

Service: Highly praised, very satisfied. There are details everywhere. There will be greetings when you enter the door. Check-in is very fast and professional, and they also help to upgrade the room.
1. TV projection. When we asked for projection, the hotel staff sent the projection equipment as soon as possible. After learning that we could not connect, they also took the initiative to provide help as soon as possible, providing high-quality services throughout the process, and finally successfully projected the screen.
2. First of all, I have stayed in no less than 10 five-star hotels in different cities in China. Few hotels will take the initiative to provide turndown service, but Nanhu Mingdu really considers and implements customer needs seriously. We went out to play and dragged our tired bodies back to the hotel. We were surprised to find that the staff opened a turndown service for us, including adjusting the lights, preparing bathrobes and anti-slip mats in advance, which is really considerate. To be honest, there are many choices of hotels at this price in Nanning. Nanhu Mingdu has done a good job in comprehensive comparison and has been providing me with surprises and warmth.
3. Did not take the initiative to ask me to give a good review. When I asked if I could upgrade the room, the staff was happy to help, but he did not ask me to give a good review on the platform, including when I checked out. It really surprised me that many hotels have the task of giving good reviews, but Nanhu Mingdu gave me the feeling that it sincerely provides customers with high-quality services, not for a good review. In my opinion, this is also one of the service details of Nanhu Mingdu.

In a word, I will choose Nanhu Mingdu again when I come to Nanning next time.

🌸Service
The staff are very enthusiastic and sunny, and respond positively. In particular, the hotel room is cleaned very well. Twice a day, two small bags of Sanpang egg melon seeds are delivered every day😂 The hotel is also soundproof, and you can't hear the sound from the next room. The hotel's breakfast is also very rich, with raw porridge, various noodles, and sour food.

🛍️Surroundings
The hotel is very close to Langxi Night Market, where there are many delicious foods. I went to several night markets and felt that Langxi was relatively large. There are also many small shops in the alleys next to the night market. There are also many delicious foods on the street behind the hotel. There is also Danggong sweet water on Shuangyong Road, which is delicious.

posted:Posted March 1, 2024
msg:Three of my relatives went to Nanning during the Spring Festival, and I must reiterate my good impression of "Nanhu Mingdu Hotel":
First, the location is good. The hotel overlooks the lake park in the city - Nanhu, and the scenery is invincible. You can go downstairs every day to visit the park, run in the morning, enjoy the scenery, and watch the lake, and enjoy the most livable urban oasis life with the locals; Nanning is not big or small, whether you go to the old city, the new district, or the mainstream attractions and commercial centers in the city, you can reach it within 5 or 6 kilometers, and all kinds of transportation are very convenient.
Second, the catering is rich, and the breakfast is very comprehensive and delicious, from local flavors to Chinese and Western cuisine, with all tastes, hygiene, quantity and service; there is a Cantonese brunch on the top floor, with a good view and a full range of tea styles. It seems that Nanning local gourmets also often visit... There are also Japanese and Western food that I haven't tried yet. In short, there is basically no complaint about the catering (only the executive lounge happy hour meal is a little inefficient, but the flaws do not cover the merits). In addition, there are various types of noodles (Laoyou noodles, snail noodles, dry noodles...) around the hotel, with countless varieties and different flavors...
Third, the hotel services and guest rooms can also reach the upper-middle level of high-star hotels, which can be regarded as thoughtful, comprehensive, patient and professional! For the many requests made by several families from morning to night: customized pillows, adding quilts in the middle of the night, heaters, searching for lost items, delayed check-out, expired administrative buildings, etc., they can respond promptly, handle them in place, and have a sincere attitude...
Fourth, for those who have the habit of fitness exercise, "Nanhu Mingdu" is even more remarkable: the five-story constant temperature infinity pool is clean and quiet, equipped with a warm water soaking pool, the locker room has a steam sauna, and there is a gym next to it... More importantly, the Nanhu Park opposite the hotel should be a holy place for local runners. It runs around the lake, the running track is well-maintained, and the scenery is suitable. The long, medium and short loops are 3, 5, and 8 kilometers respectively, which are suitable for all types of runners. There are lake lights, tree shadows, bridges and embankments, and flowers. If you are hungry and tired, there are teahouses and coffees everywhere around, and breakfast tea meals... Tourists are suitable for all ages...
Therefore, living in Nanhu Mingdu can be said to have the best urban resources and cultural environment in Nanning. If you are a typical senior hotel control, I believe that you can relax your mind and stay for a few days in one store, one place, and one environment here, and it will not be boring...

msg:來南寧玩，想要住的舒服一點，提前在攜程上定了他家的商務雙人房。房間很大，衞生也很乾凈，乾濕分離，還有個浴缸可以舒服的泡澡，晚上還可以看到夜景，挺美的。服務也很好，正好去的時候感冒了，每天都有外賣送葯送粥本來就送到樓下，但是打電話了都願意幫我送上門，行李也有專人拿上去，出去遊玩身體突然不適，但是還有被温暖到。

早餐的品種挺豐富，因為這裡是有專門的粵菜館，所以我覺得早餐最好吃的就是包子，豬肝粥，感冒吃這些熱乎的最好了。

機場過來可以做2號線到沃頓酒店，下來20分鐘，地鐵的話也步行這點時間，門口公交車直達市區的各個景點。

msg:這是家僅看名字和攜程房間照片就很容易忽略的好酒店，要不是老家南寧的朋友力薦差點就錯過了，酒店裝修和名字一樣中規中矩沒有太多特色，但配套特別齊全，力量器械均為Life Fitness的健身房、水質清潔的泳池、Spa等應有盡有，50樓的湖庭中餐廳粵式早茶確實像好友説的那麼棒，黑色的榴蓮酥讓我想起了以前在廣州白天鵝賓館玉堂春暖和宏圖府餐廳的天鵝酥，菜品份量超過我的預期而且並不貴，酒店最棒的就是對面的南湖公園，每天都要去裡邊轉兩圈，很像過去去過的中科院西雙版納植物園和公園的混合體，值得一提的是酒店後面小街有很多小餐館，可以嚐到地道的南寧老友粉等，住了幾天唯一覺得遺憾的就是玻璃幕牆很久沒清洗過，影響觀看南湖公園美景，但如果下次再去南寧，這家酒店是不二之選。（這是我用攜程以來評價字數最多的一家酒店）

msg:房間景觀：
本地的品牌酒店，緊靠南湖位置很好，行政雙床房間的視野也不錯，可以看到南湖和城景。我個人更喜歡湖景房的view，更漂亮。
剛入酒店的時候服務人員態度很好很熱情，但是第二天告知房卡衹做了一天，好在及時更正。
房間設施：
房間就是五星標準的配置，拖鞋，床品，毛巾，洗髮水等品質都不錯，感覺比香格里拉的好。
游泳池：
挺大挺乾淨的
位置交通：
我們都打車出行，位置挺方便的
早餐：
中規中矩
性價比：
行政雙床房含行政禮遇（兩個早餐，兩份下午茶，兩份歡樂時光，歡樂時光是可以點菜的那種）600多的價格我覺得性價比很可以。
五星推薦

msg:酒店服務太差，我和愛人都是七十多歲的人，晚上想在酒店吃個便飯，入住前打電話詢問前台服務員説有中餐吃，我們才訂了該酒店，但到酒店後中餐廳沒有散客座位:服務員讓我們去包間。去包間後我們點了一個檸檬鴨一個素菜，直到我們吃完飯了，素菜也沒上來。服務員還強行要給我們上茶水，每人8元，我們説年紀大了喝茶水晚上睡不着覺，更何況我是房顫患者，醫生要求不能喝茶。但服務員堅持要按8元一人收費，並改口説是餐具費.我當即反駁説吃飯不提供餐具難道讓客人從鍋裏抓着吃嗎？.後又來一服務員説這是店裡的規定:我説你們店裡的規定不合情不合理不合法，你們的規定強制客人出錢完成是**邏輯。經反覆爭吵，最後沒有收這茶水費。我感覺該酒店象***的黑店。我在攜程上訂的是全江景房，到店後前台卻説我是用了積分優惠，給我開了一間普通房，真是不講理。優惠是攜程對鉑金客户的優惠，酒店可以隨意取消，這鉑金客户的優惠豈不成了忽悠人的圈套。希望攜程對此事能有一個明確的説法。總之，這個酒店完全不具備五星酒店的服務，希望大家看到我的經歷後慎重選擇該酒店，以免被宰。

在48樓餐廳吃了早茶，菜品不錯，價格也不高，衹是服務差強人意，整個用餐過程沒有人給茶續水，也沒有來更換過明顯已裝滿的骨碟。
最讓人不滿和值得吐槽的是房間衹給了兩瓶飲用水。打電話請前台再送幾瓶水，告知我需要收費，免費的衹提供兩瓶……五星酒店，七八百的房價，住了全國無數個酒店，還真是第一次。讓人無語，再説其他都是徒勞！
除了南湖景觀，毫無可取之處，這個價格，南寧可供選擇的品牌酒店實在太多！
